Task instruction sent to agent 
# Implement HyperLogLog Algorithm

**Repository:** bustub (TheAgentCompany GitLab)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** ccb_tac
**Task Type:** Algorithm Implementation

## Description

Implement the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the
bustub database system. This requires understanding the existing codebase structure,
following coding conventions, and implementing the algorithm across 4 files.

## Task

Clone http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace folder and complete
http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub/-/issues/759 locally.

Specifically, complete 4 files:
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`

To ensure compatibility of testing across different operating systems, please change
the line `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` in your local file
`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h` to:
`hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully
[x] All 4 implementation files completed
[x] Unit tests pass (10 tests, graded by pass count)

## Notes

- This task uses TheAgentCompany's pre-built environment
- Deterministic grading via unit tests
- Score is based on number of passing tests (each test worth 0.5 points)

    23→namespace bustub {
    24→
    25→using hash_t = std::size_t;
    26→
    27→class HashUtil {
    28→ private:
    29→  static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;
    30→
    31→ public:
    32→  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    33→    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126
    34→    hash_t hash = length;
    35→    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
    36→      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];
    37→    }
    38→    return hash;
    39→  }
    40→
    41→  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    42→    hash_t both[2] = {};
    43→    both[0] = l;
    44→    both[1] = r;
    45→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);
    46→  }
    47→
    48→  static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    49→    return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;
    50→  }
    51→
    52→  template <typename T>
    53→  static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
    54→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_c
... (truncated)

     5→template <typename KeyType>
     6→HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
     7→  if (n_bits <= 0) {
     8→    m_ = 0;
     9→  } else {
    10→    m_ = 1ULL << n_bits;
    11→    registers_.assign(m_, 0);
    12→  }
    13→}
    14→
    15→template <typename KeyType>
    16→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
    17→  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);
    18→}
    19→
    20→template <typename KeyType>
    21→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
    22→  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (rho function)
    23→  // Return 1 + number of leading zero bits
    24→  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    25→    if (bset[i]) {
    26→      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i;
    27→    }
    28→  }
    29→  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;
    30→}
    31→
    32→template <typename KeyType>
    33→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
    34→  if (m_ == 0) {
    35→    return;
    36→  }
    37→
    38→  // Hash the element
    39→  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);
    40→
    41→  // Extract bucket index using the first n_bits
    42→  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_bits_) - 1);
    43→
    44→  // Get the remaining bits by shifting
    45→  hash_t w = hash >> n_bits_;
    46→
    47→  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits
    48→  auto bset = ComputeBinary(w);
    49→  uint64_t leftmost_one_pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bset);

Review all changed files for reuse, quality, and efficiency. Fix any issues found.

## Phase 1: Identify Changes

Run `git diff` (or `git diff HEAD` if there are staged changes) to see what changed. If there are no git changes, review the most recently modified files that the user mentioned or that you edited earlier in this conversation.

Use the Agent tool to launch all three agents concurrently in a single message. Pass each agent the full diff so it has the complete context.

### Agent 1: Code Reuse Review

For each change:

1. **Search for existing utilities and helpers** that could replace newly written code. Use Grep to find similar patterns elsewhere in the codebase — common locations are utility directories, shared modules, and files adjacent to the changed ones.
2. **Flag any new function that duplicates existing functionality.** Suggest the existing function to use instead.
3. **Flag any inline logic that could use an existing utility** — hand-rolled string manipulation, manual path handling, custom environment checks, ad-hoc type guards, and similar patterns are common candidates.

1. **Redundant state**: state that duplicates existing state, cached values that could be derived, observers/effects that could be direct calls
2. **Parameter sprawl**: adding new parameters to a function instead of generalizing or restructuring existing ones
3. **Copy-paste with slight variation**: near-duplicate code blocks that should be unified with a shared abstraction
4. **Leaky abstractions**: exposing internal details that should be encapsulated, or breaking existing abstraction boundaries

Let me analyze the test failures more carefully. Looking at the test cases, I notice an important pattern in the PrestoCase tests that tells me how the encoding should work.

Let me trace through a specific test case to understand the encoding:

For `PrestoCase1` with `n_leading_bits=1` and `AddElem(262144)`:
- 262144 = 0x40000 in binary
- With n_leading_bits=1: j = 262144 & 1 = 0, w = 262144 >> 1 = 131072
- 131072 = 0x20000, the first 1 bit is at position 17 (counting from 0)
- rho = 17 + 1 = 18
- Expected: dense=2, overflow=1
- If dense = rho & 0xF = 18 & 15 = 2 ✓, overflow = rho >> 4 = 1 ✓

This confirms my logic for splitting rho is correct. However, I need to review my implementation more carefully. Let me check if there's an issue with the constants or boundaries used in the Presto version:

142-usertool_resultRead
    17→
    18→template <typename KeyType>
    19→auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
    20→  if (m_ == 0) {
    21→    return;
    22→  }
    23→
    24→  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);
    25→
    26→  // Extract bucket index using first n_leading_bits
    27→  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);
    28→
    29→  // Get remaining bits
    30→  hash_t w = hash >> n_leading_bits_;
    31→
    32→  // Calculate position of leftmost one in remaining bits
    33→  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(w);
    34→
    35→  // Store in dense/overflow buckets
    36→  if (rho <= 15) {
    37→    // Fits in dense bucket (4 bits can store 0-15)
    38→    uint64_t current = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
    39→    dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current, rho));
    40→  } else {
    41→    // Need overflow bucket
    42→    uint64_t dense_part = rho & 0xFULL;  // Lower 4 bits
    43→    uint64_t overflow_part = rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits
    44→
    45→    // Update dense with max
    46→    uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
    47→    dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_dense, dense_part));
    48→
    49→    // Update overflow with max
    50→    if (overflow_bucket_.find(j) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
    51→      uint64_t current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
    52→      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_overflow, overflow_part));
    53→    } else {
    54→      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_part);
    55→    }
    56→  }

Looking at the expected cardinality of 3 with just one element, I think untouched buckets should contribute `2^(-0)=1` to the sum, which means `rho=0` for untouched buckets. But if we store `(rho-1)`, then `rho=1` would give `encoded=0`. So for untouched buckets that have `dense=0`, we should treat them as `rho=0`, not `rho=1`.

     6→template <typename KeyType>
     7→HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
     8→  if (n_bits <= 0) {
     9→    m_ = 0;
    10→  } else {
    11→    m_ = 1ULL << n_bits;
    12→    registers_.assign(m_, 0);
    13→  }
    14→}
    15→
    16→template <typename KeyType>
    17→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
    18→  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);
    19→}
    20→
    21→template <typename KeyType>
    22→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
    23→  // Count trailing zeros and add 1
    24→  // This is the rho function: position of first 1 bit counting from the right
    25→  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; ++i) {
    26→    if (bset[i]) {
    27→      return i + 1;
    28→    }
    29→  }
    30→  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;
    31→}
    32→
    33→template <typename KeyType>
    34→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
    35→  if (m_ == 0) {
    36→    return;
    37→  }
    38→
    39→  // Hash the element
    40→  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);
    41→
    42→  // Extract bucket index using the first n_bits
    43→  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_bits_) - 1);
    44→
    45→  // Get the remaining bits by shifting
    46→  hash_t w = hash >> n_bits_;
    47→
    48→  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits
    49→  auto bset = ComputeBinary(w);
    50→  uint64_t leftmost_one_pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bset);
    51→
    52→  // Update register with maximum value
    53→  registers_[j] = std::max(registers_[j
... (truncated)

i < m_; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow\n      // dense stores lower 4 bits, overflow stores higher bits\n      uint64_t rho = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));\n    } else {\n      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(dense_val));\n    }\n  }\n\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Count leading zeros from the left + 1\n  // If val is 0, return 65\n  if (val == 0) {\n    return 65;\n  }\n  // Use __builtin_clzll to count leading zeros (only works for 64-bit)\n  return 65 - __builtin_clzll(val);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i < m_; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t rho;\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow\n      // We stored (rho-1), so reconstruct it\n      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n      rho = encoded + 1;\n    } else if (dense_val == 0) {\n      // Untouched bucket: treat as rho=0\n      rho = 0;\n    } else {\n      // Dense only: the value is (rho-1), so rho = dense_val + 1\n      rho = dense_val + 1;\n    }\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));\n  }\n\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Count trailing zeros and add 1\n  // This is the rho function: position of first 1 bit from the right\n  if (val == 0) {\n    return 65;\n  }\n  // Use __builtin_ctzll to count trailing zeros\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(__builtin_ctzll(val)) + 1;\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i < m_; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t rho;\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow\n      // We stored (rho-1), so reconstruct it\n      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n      rho = encoded + 1;\n    } else if (dense_val == 0) {\n      // Untouched bucket: treat as rho=0\n      rho = 0;\n    } else {\n      // Dense only: the value is (rho-1), so rho = dense_val + 1\n      rho = dense_val + 1;\n    }\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));\n  }\n\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Count trailing zeros and add 1\n  // This is the rho function: position of first 1 bit from the right\n  if (val == 0) {\n    return 65;\n  }\n  // Use __builtin_ctzll to count trailing zeros\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(__builtin_ctzll(val)) + 1;\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i < m_; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t rho;\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow\n      // We store rho directly, so reconstruct it\n      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n      rho = encoded;\n    } else if (dense_val == 0) {\n      // Untouched bucket: treat as rho=0\n      rho = 0;\n    } else {\n      // Dense only: the value is rho stored directly\n      rho = dense_val;\n    }\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));\n  }\n\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Count trailing zeros and add 1\n  // This is the rho function: position of first 1 bit from the right\n  if (val == 0) {\n    return 65;\n  }\n  // Use __builtin_ctzll to count trailing zeros\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(__builtin_ctzll(val)) + 1;\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (rho function)
  // Return 1 + number of leading zero bits
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;
}
6. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>

  /** @TODO(student) Implement this function! */

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Hash the element
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index using the first n_bits
  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_bits_) - 1);

  // Get the remaining bits by shifting
  hash_t w = hash >> n_bits_;

  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits
  auto bset = ComputeBinary(w);
  uint64_t leftmost_one_pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bset);

  // Update register with maximum value
  registers_[j] = std::max(registers_[j], static_cast<uint8_t>(leftmost_one_pos));
}

After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  // Calculate the raw estimate
  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {
    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;

  // Cast to uint64_t
  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);
}

    m_ = 0;
  } else {

10. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  /** @TODO(student) Implement this function! */
}

template class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;
template class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;
}  // namespace bustub
After
template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {
    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();

    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow
      // dense stores lower 4 bits, overflow stores higher bits
      uint64_t rho = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));
    } else {
      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(dense_val));
    }
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;
  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {
  // Count leading zeros from the left + 1
  // If val is 0, return 65
  if (val == 0) {
    return 65;
  }
  // Use __builtin_clzll to count leading zeros (only works for 64-bit)
  return 65 - __builtin_clzll(val);
}

template class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;
template class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;
}  // namespace bustub
11. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  /** @TODO(student) Implement this function! */
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index using first n_leading_bits
  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Get remaining bits
  hash_t w = hash >> n_leading_bits_;

  // Calculate position of leftmost one in remaining bits
  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(w);

  // Store in dense/overflow buckets
  if (rho <= 15) {
    // Fits in dense bucket (4 bits can store 0-15)
    uint64_t current = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
    dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current, rho));
  } else {
    // Need overflow bucket
    uint64_t dense_part = rho & 0xFULL;  // Lower 4 bits
    uint64_t overflow_part = rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits

    // Update dense with max
    uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
    dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_dense, dense_part));

    // Update overflow with max
    if (overflow_bucket_.find(j) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_overflow, overflow_part));
    } else {
      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_part);
    }
  }
}

14. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (rho function)
  // Return 1 + number of leading zero bits
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Count trailing zeros and add 1
  // This is the rho function: position of first 1 bit counting from the right
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY; ++i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return i + 1;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;
}
15. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {
  // Count leading zeros from the left + 1
  // If val is 0, return 65
  if (val == 0) {
    return 65;
  }
  // Use __builtin_clzll to count leading zeros (only works for 64-bit)
  return 65 - __builtin_clzll(val);
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash_t val) const -> uint64_t {
  // Count trailing zeros and add 1
  // This is the rho function: position of first 1 bit from the right
  if (val == 0) {
    return 65;
  }
  // Use __builtin_ctzll to count trailing zeros
  return static_cast<uint64_t>(__builtin_ctzll(val)) + 1;
}

17. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {
    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();

    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow
      // dense stores lower 4 bits, overflow stores higher bits
      uint64_t rho = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));
    } else {
      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(dense_val));
    }
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;
  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);
}
After
template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {
    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    uint64_t rho;

    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow
      // We stored (rho-1), so reconstruct it
      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
      rho = encoded + 1;
    } else {
      // Dense only: the value is (rho-1), so rho = dense_val + 1
      rho = dense_val + 1;
    }
    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;
  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);
}
18. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index using first n_leading_bits
  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Get remaining bits
  hash_t w = hash >> n_leading_bits_;

  // Calculate position of leftmost one in remaining bits
  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(w);

  // Store in dense/overflow buckets
  // Presto encoding: store (rho-1) split into dense and overflow
  uint64_t encoded_rho = rho - 1;
  uint64_t dense_part = encoded_rho & 0xFULL;  // Lower 4 bits
  uint64_t overflow_part = encoded_rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits

  // Update dense with max
  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
  dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_dense, dense_part));

  // Update overflow with max if we have overflow bits
  if (overflow_part > 0) {
    if (overflow_bucket_.find(j) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_overflow, overflow_part));
    } else {
      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_part);
    }
  }
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index using first n_leading_bits
  uint64_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Calculate rho from the full hash value
  // rho is the position of the first 1-bit (trailing zeros + 1)
  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(hash);

  // Store in dense/overflow buckets
  // Presto encoding: store (rho-1) split into dense and overflow
  uint64_t encoded_rho = rho - 1;
  uint64_t dense_part = encoded_rho & 0xFULL;  // Lower 4 bits
  uint64_t overflow_part = encoded_rho >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;  // Upper bits

  // Update dense with max
  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
  dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_dense, dense_part));

  // Update overflow with max if we have overflow bits
  if (overflow_part > 0) {
    if (overflow_bucket_.find(j) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[j].to_ullong();
      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(std::max(current_overflow, overflow_part));
    } else {
      overflow_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_part);
    }
  }
}

template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {

    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {

    uint64_t rho;

      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow
      // We stored (rho-1), so reconstruct it
      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
      rho = encoded + 1;
    } else {
      // Dense only: the value is (rho-1), so rho = dense_val + 1
      rho = dense_val + 1;
    }
    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;

    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;

    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;

template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {
    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    uint64_t rho;

    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow
      // We stored (rho-1), split across dense and overflow
      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
      rho = encoded + 1;

      // Re-store the reconstructed rho in normalized form
      uint64_t new_encoded = rho - 1;
      uint64_t new_dense = new_encoded & 0xFULL;
      uint64_t new_overflow = new_encoded >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;
      dense_bucket_[i] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);
      overflow_bucket_[i] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_overflow);
    } else if (dense_val == 0) {
      // Untouched bucket: treat as rho=0
      rho = 0;
    } else {
      // Dense only: the value is (rho-1), so rho = dense_val + 1
      rho = dense_val + 1;

      // Re-store the reconstructed rho in normalized form
      uint64_t new_encoded = rho - 1;
      uint64_t new_dense = new_encoded & 0xFULL;
      dense_bucket_[i] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);
    }
    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;
  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);
}

template <typename T>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (m_ == 0) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  double sum = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < m_; ++i) {
    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
    uint64_t rho;

    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {
      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();
      // Reconstruct rho from dense and overflow
      // We stored (rho-1), split across dense and overflow
      uint64_t encoded = dense_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);
      rho = encoded + 1;
    } else if (dense_val == 0) {
      // Untouched bucket: treat as rho=0
      rho = 0;
    } else {
      // Dense only: the value is (rho-1), so rho = dense_val + 1
      rho = dense_val + 1;
    }
    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));
  }

  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m_) * static_cast<double>(m_) / sum;
  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);
